Finally- an important trick to knowing whether you are receiving a first rate product: This product comes in a bottle which lights up with little LED lights. Twice I got a new bottle with the battery protecting tag still in place. I pulled it out and little lights around the front label blink for about ten seconds. On the other occasion the tag was not in place and the battery was dead. Just food for thought if you're looking for the highest quality merchandise. In short- Great product. Just watch the price and keep in mind that you may not be getting a new bottle.
